<p>This page contains information about all <b>342 languages</b> for which official <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedias</a> have been created under the auspices of the <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation" title="Wikimedia Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a>. The table below, however, excludes <a href="#Closed_and_read-only">13 Wikipedias that were closed</a> and moved to the <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="incubator:">Wikimedia Incubator</a> for further development, leaving a current total of <b>329</b> active Wikipedias. Content in other languages is being developed at the Wikimedia Incubator; languages which meet <a href="/wiki/Language_proposal_policy" title="Language proposal policy">certain criteria</a> can get their own <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/wiki" class="extiw" title="w:wiki">wikis</a>.
</p><p>The table entries are ordered by current article count. Each entry gives the language name in English (linked to the English Wikipedia article for the language); its "local name" (i.e. in the language itself, linked to the article in that language's wiki); the <a href="/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix" title="Special:SiteMatrix">language code</a> used in the wiki's <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/URL" class="extiw" title="w:URL">URL</a> address and in <a href="/wiki/Help:Interwiki_linking" title="Help:Interwiki linking">interwiki links</a> to it (linked to the local Main Page); and statistics on articles, edits, administrators, users, active users, and images (each linked to an appropriate local special page).
</p><p>To start a Wikipedia in a new language, please see our <a href="/wiki/Language_proposal_policy" title="Language proposal policy">language proposal policy</a> and <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:Manual" class="extiw" title="incubator:Help:Manual">the Incubator manual</a>. <b>Note: Just adding a link here does not create a new Wikipedia, nor does it serve to request that one be created.</b>
</p><p>If a wiki becomes active and is not listed here, please post a notice on <a href="/wiki/Talk:List_of_Wikipedias" title="Talk:List of Wikipedias">this article's talk page</a>, including a link to <i>all</i> the relevant Wikipedia pages, and help promote the effort by announcing it on the <a href="/wiki/Mailing_lists/Overview#Project_mailing_lists" title="Mailing lists/Overview">Wikipedia-L</a> mailing list, and at <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_News" title="Wikimedia News">Wikimedia News</a>.
</p><p><b>The tables here are maintained automatically</b> based on statistics collected by a bot four times a day, so <b>it is not necessary to "manually" update the table.</b> (The way this is being done makes that impossible, anyway.) If something is wrong with an entry other than simply having slightly outdated statistics, post about it on the <a href="/wiki/Talk:List_of_Wikipedias" title="Talk:List of Wikipedias">talk page</a>.
</p><p><b>More lists of Wikipedias by various criteria :</b> <small class="noprint"> [ <span style="font-size: smaller"><a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Template:Lists_of_Wikipedias" title="Special:EditPage/Template:Lists of Wikipedias">edit</a></span> ]</small>
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-selflink selflink">List of Wikipedias</a> by <b>article count</b>, <b>users</b>, <b>file count</b> and <b>depth</b> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wikistats.wmcloud.org/display.php?t=wp">its source</a> <small>(both updated every 6 hours)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_edits_per_article" title="List of Wikipedias by edits per article">List of Wikipedias by <b>edits</b> per article</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_article_depth" title="Wikipedia article depth">depth</a> <small>(both updated every 6 hours)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_language_group" title="List of Wikipedias by language group">List of Wikipedias by <b>language</b> group</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_language_family" title="List of Wikipedias by language family">family</a> <small>(both updated every 6 hours)</small> and <a href="/wiki/Tree_of_Wikimedia_wikis_by_language_family" title="Tree of Wikimedia wikis by language family">language families as a tree</a> <small>(not just Wikipedias)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_country" title="List of Wikipedias by country">List of Wikipedias by <b>country</b></a> <small>(updated manually)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_speakers_per_article" title="List of Wikipedias by speakers per article">List of Wikipedias by <b>speakers</b> per article</a> <small>(updated every 6 hours)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_sample_of_articles" title="List of Wikipedias by sample of articles">List of Wikipedias by <b>sample</b> of articles</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_expanded_sample_of_articles" title="List of Wikipedias by expanded sample of articles">expanded sample of articles</a> <small>(both updated monthly)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_featured_articles" title="Wikipedia featured articles">List of Wikipedias by <b>featured</b></a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_good_articles" title="Wikipedia good articles"><b>good</b> articles</a><small> (both updated manually)</small></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Anniversary" class="extiw" title="en:Wikipedia:Anniversary">List of Wikipedias by <b>creation date</b></a> <small>(incomplete)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedias_in_multiple_writing_systems" title="Wikipedias in multiple writing systems">List of Wikipedias in <b>multiple writing systems</b></a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_local_media_files" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Wikipedias having local media files">List of Wikipedias having <b>local media files</b></a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_zero_local_media_files" title="List of Wikipedias having zero local media files">zero local media files</a> <small>(both updated manually)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_milestones" title="Wikipedia milestones">List of Wikipedia <b>milestones</b></a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Milestone_statistics" class="extiw" title="en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics">en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics</a> <small>(tracking of major article-count milestones)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_wikis" title="List of largest wikis">List of largest wikis</a> <small>(not just Wikimedia wikis)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_News" title="Wikimedia News">Wikimedia News</a> <small>(announcements and tracking of milestones for all Wikimedia projects)</small></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tell_us_about_your_Wikipedia" title="Tell us about your Wikipedia">Tell us about your Wikipedia</a></li></ul>
</section><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2 ext-discussiontools-init-section section-heading" onclick="mfTempOpenSection(1)"><span class="indicator mf-icon mf-icon-expand mf-icon--small"></span><h2 data-mw-thread-id="h-Notes"><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Notes"></span>Notes<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Notes"></span></span></h2><!--__DTELLIPSISBUTTON__{"threadItem":{"headingLevel":2,"name":"h-","type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Notes","replies":[]}}--></div><section class="mf-section-1 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-1">
<ul><li>The "<b>All pages</b>" column refers to the number of pages in <i>all</i> namespaces, including both <b>articles</b> (the <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:Article_count" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:Article count">official article count</a> of each wiki) and <b>non-articles</b> (user pages, images, talk pages, "project" pages, categories, and templates).</li>
<li>"<b>Active Users</b>" are registered users who have made at least one edit in the last thirty days.</li>
<li>"<b>Files</b>" is the number of locally uploaded files. Note that some large Wikipedias do not use local images or other media files and rely on <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons" title="Wikimedia Commons">Commons</a> completely, so the value "0" is not a glitch (see also <a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_zero_local_media_files" title="List of Wikipedias having zero local media files">List of Wikipedias having zero local media files</a>).</li></ul>
</section><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2 ext-discussiontools-init-section section-heading" onclick="mfTempOpenSection(2)"><span class="indicator mf-icon mf-icon-expand mf-icon--small"></span><h2 data-mw-thread-id="h-All_Wikipedias_ordered_by_number_of_articles"><span class="mw-headline" id="All_Wikipedias_ordered_by_number_of_articles"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-All_Wikipedias_ordered_by_number_of_articles"></span><span id="table"></span>All Wikipedias ordered by number of articles<span data-mw-comment-end="h-All_Wikipedias_ordered_by_number_of_articles"></span></span></h2><!--__DTELLIPSISBUTTON__{"threadItem":{"headingLevel":2,"name":"h-","type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-All_Wikipedias_ordered_by_number_of_articles","replies":[]}}--></div><section class="mf-section-2 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-2">
<p>The languages listed here are Wikipedias that have been created as separate subdomains of wikipedia.org, ordered by number of <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:Article_count" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:Article count">articles</a>. The table can also be sorted by other columns. It excludes <a href="#Closed_and_read-only">closed Wikipedias</a>. Historical data of this table dating back to 2007 can be found in the <a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedias/Table&amp;action=history">history of this table</a> (or, after 15 October 2022, in the <a class="external text" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data:Wikipedia_statistics/data.tab&amp;action=history">history of the current source of the data</a>).
</p>
<dl><dd><i>These statistics are updated four times a day. See <a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Data:Wikipedia_statistics/data.tab" class="extiw" title="commons:Data:Wikipedia statistics/data.tab">commons:Data:Wikipedia statistics/data.tab</a> for the date/time of last update. (If reloading this page doesn't update the numbers to what is seen at Commons, try <a href="/wiki/Special:Purge/List_of_Wikipedias" title="Special:Purge/List of Wikipedias">purging the cache</a>.)</i></dd></dl>

</section><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2 ext-discussiontools-init-section section-heading" onclick="mfTempOpenSection(3)"><span class="indicator mf-icon mf-icon-expand mf-icon--small"></span><h2 data-mw-thread-id="h-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Wikipedias"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Deprecated,_moved_and_other"></span> Other Wikipedias<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h2><!--__DTELLIPSISBUTTON__{"threadItem":{"headingLevel":2,"name":"h-","type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Other_Wikipedias","replies":["h-Not_yet_created-Other_Wikipedias","h-Closed_and_read-only-Other_Wikipedias","h-Deleted_but_hosted_elsewhere-Other_Wikipedias","h-Nonstandard_language_codes-Other_Wikipedias","h-Redirects-Other_Wikipedias","h-Non-language_subdomains-Other_Wikipedias"]}}--></div><section class="mf-section-3 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-3">
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Not_yet_created-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Not_yet_created"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Not_yet_created-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Test_Wikipedias"></span> Not yet created<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Not_yet_created-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<p>Please visit the <b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="incubator:">Wikimedia Incubator</a></b> for new language versions (known as "tests") that may become stand-alone wikis in the future. See the Incubator <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:Manual" class="extiw" title="incubator:Help:Manual">Manual</a> and <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:FAQ" class="extiw" title="incubator:Help:FAQ">FAQ</a> for more information.
</p>
<ul><li><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Template:Tests/wp" class="extiw" title="incubator:Template:Tests/wp">Manually maintained list of test Wikipedias</a> in the Incubator</li>
<li><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:SearchWiki" class="extiw" title="incubator:Special:SearchWiki">Search for a wiki</a> in over 400 different languages (includes normal Wikipedias and test Wikipedias)</li></ul>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Closed_and_read-only-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Closed_and_read-only"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Closed_and_read-only-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Read-only"></span> Closed and read-only<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Closed_and_read-only-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<p>These Wikipedias are closed and in read-only status. Existing users can still log in and their user preferences are still effective, but they cannot edit any pages. Editiable copies of these Wikipedias can be found in the Incubator; for example, the page <a href="https://cho.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chahta" class="extiw" title="cho:Chahta">cho:Chahta</a> at the closed Choctaw Wikipedia can be found (and edited) at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cho/Chahta" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/cho/Chahta">incubator:Wp/cho/Chahta</a>.
</p>
<ol><li><a href="https://aa.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="aa:">aa:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Afar language">Afar</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Afar_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Afar Wikipedia">closed on 10 May 2008</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/aa" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/aa">incubator:Wp/aa</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://ak.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ak:">ak:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akan language">Akan</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Akan_Wikipedia_2" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Akan Wikipedia 2">closed on 1 April 2023</a>. It should be noted that Akan is now considered a family of languages, so the ak.wikipedia domain has been split into two separate projects (and potentially more): one for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twi" class="extiw" title="w:Twi">Twi</a> at <a href="https://tw.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="tw:">tw:</a>, and another for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fante_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Fante dialect">Fante</a> at <a href="https://fat.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="fat:">fat:</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://cho.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="cho:">cho:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Choctaw_language" class="extiw" title="w:Choctaw language">Choctaw</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Choctaw_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Choctaw Wikipedia">closed on 3 July 2007</a>, following a community vote. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cho" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/cho">incubator:Wp/cho</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://ho.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ho:">ho:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiri_Motu" class="extiw" title="w:Hiri Motu">Hiri Motu</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Hiri_Motu_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Hiri Motu Wikipedia">closed on 9 July 2007</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ho" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ho">incubator:Wp/ho</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://hz.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="hz:">hz:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herero_language" class="extiw" title="w:Herero language">Herero</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Herero_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Herero Wikipedia">closed on 24 July 2007</a>. The wiki has been emptied and locked, but the original user pages still exist. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/hz" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/hz">incubator:Wp/hz</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://ii.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ii:">ii:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuosu_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nuosu language">Yi</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Yi_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Yi Wikipedia">closed on 29 July 2007</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ii" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ii">incubator:Wp/ii</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://kj.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="kj:">kj:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kwanyama_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Kwanyama dialect">Kwanyama</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Kwanyama_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Kwanyama Wikipedia">closed on 10 July 2007</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kj" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/kj">incubator:Wp/kj</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://kr.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="kr:">kr:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanuri_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kanuri language">Kanuri</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Kanuri_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Kanuri Wikipedia">closed on 3 May 2007</a>, following a community vote. The reason was the absence of both content and community. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kr" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/kr">incubator:Wp/kr</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://lrc.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="lrc:">lrc:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Luri_language" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Luri language">Northern Luri</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Northern_Luri_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Northern Luri Wikipedia">closed on 14 January 2021</a>. As almost all of the former contents were confirmed not written in proper Luri, they were not imported back into the Incubator. Users who speak the language are encouraged to re-start <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/lrc" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/lrc">a test project</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://mh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mh:">mh:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marshallese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Marshallese language">Marshallese</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Marshallese_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Marshallese Wikipedia">closed on 4 May 2008</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mh" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/mh">incubator:Wp/mh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://mus.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mus:">mus:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muscogee_language" class="extiw" title="w:Muscogee language">Muscogee</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Muscogee_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Muscogee Wikipedia">closed on 10 July 2007</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mus" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/mus">incubator:Wp/mus</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://na.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="na:">na:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nauruan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nauruan language">Nauruan</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Nauruan_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Nauruan Wikipedia">closed on 1 May 2023</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/na" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/na">incubator:Wp/na</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://ng.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ng:">ng:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ndonga_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Ndonga dialect">Ndonga</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Ndonga_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Ndonga Wikipedia">closed on 10 January 2010</a>. It is now found at <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ng" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ng">incubator:Wp/ng</a>.</li></ol>
<p>See also our <a href="/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix" title="Special:SiteMatrix">Special:SiteMatrix</a>, where the closed Wikipedias are crossed out (and the red links indicate wikis that have never existed). There is also a configuration file listing <a class="external text" href="https://noc.wikimedia.org/conf/highlight.php?file=dblists/closed.dblist">all closed Wikimedia projects</a>.
</p>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Deleted_but_hosted_elsewhere-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Deleted_but_hosted_elsewhere"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Deleted_but_hosted_elsewhere-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Moved_and_deleted"></span> Deleted but hosted elsewhere<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Deleted_but_hosted_elsewhere-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<p>These Wikipedias are no longer hosted by Wikimedia. They have been moved to other hosts.
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Tok:&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tok: (page does not exist)">tok:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toki_Pona" class="extiw" title="w:Toki Pona">Toki Pona</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Tokipona_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Tokipona Wikipedia">officially closed in 2008</a> and all projects in that language were <a href="https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T13511" class="extiw" title="phab:T13511">deleted in 2010</a> due to the lack of a valid ISO language code. The wiki was hosted by Wikia (which became <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fandom_(website)" class="extiw" title="w:Fandom (website)">Fandom</a>) until 2021. It is now an independently hosted encyclopedia at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://wikipesija.org">https://wikipesija.org</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Tlh:&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tlh: (page does not exist)">tlh:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Klingon_language" class="extiw" title="w:Klingon language">Klingon</a> Wikipedia was permanently locked in August 2005, and was moved to Wikia (Fandom) as the <a href="https://community.fandom.com/wiki/w:c:Klingon" class="extiw" title="wikia:Klingon">Klingon Wiki</a>. For details, see the <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Klingon_Wikipedia" title="History of the Klingon Wikipedia">history of the Klingon Wikipedia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ru-sib:&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ru-sib: (page does not exist)">ru-sib:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siberian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Siberian language">Siberian</a> Wikipedia was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Deletion_of_Siberian_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Deletion of Siberian Wikipedia">deleted in 2007</a> after it became apparent that the creation of the wiki in 2006 was based on a hoax. The wiki's content was moved to the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://yauzaforum.ru/upliner/sibvolgota/">sibvolgota</a> (now a dead link).</li>
<li><a href="https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mo:">mo:</a> – The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Moldovan language">Moldovan</a> Wikipedia in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_Cyrillic_alphabet" class="extiw" title="w:Moldovan Cyrillic alphabet">Moldovan Cyrillic alphabet</a> was <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Deletion_of_Moldovan_Wikipedia_2" title="Proposals for closing projects/Deletion of Moldovan Wikipedia 2">deleted in November 2017</a>, a decade after being <a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Moldovan_Wikipedia" title="Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Moldovan Wikipedia">closed</a>. It is now hosted by Fandom as <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wpmo.fandom.com/mo/wiki/%D0%9F%D0%B0%D3%82%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BD%D1%87%D0%B8%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BB%D1%8D">Википедия</a>. The <a href="https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mo:">mo:</a> interlanguage prefix now points to the Romanian Wikipedia.</li></ol>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Nonstandard_language_codes-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Nonstandard_language_codes"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Nonstandard_language_codes-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Deprecated"></span><span id="Deprecated_language_codes"></span> Nonstandard language codes<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Nonstandard_language_codes-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<p>These Wikipedias use language codes that do not conform to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_639" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 639">ISO 639</a> standard (which is how wiki subdomains are chosen nowadays).
</p>
<ol><li><a href="https://als.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="als:">als:</a> – originally used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alsatian_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Alsatian dialect">Alsatian</a> Wikipedia, which now encompasses the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alemannic_German" class="extiw" title="w:Alemannic German">Alemannic dialects</a> in general — the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/gsw">gsw</a></code> is being considered as a replacement subdomain (note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/als">als</a></code> officially represents the unrelated language <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tosk_Albanian" class="extiw" title="w:Tosk Albanian">Tosk Albanian</a>)</li>
<li><a href="https://bat-smg.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bat-smg:">bat-smg:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samogitian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Samogitian language">Samogitian</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/sgs">sgs</a></code>)</li>
<li><a href="https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="be-tarask:">be-tarask:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tara%C5%A1kievica" class="extiw" title="w:Taraškievica">Belarusian (Taraškievica)</a> Wikipedia, combination of <code>be</code> for Belarusian and IETF language tag <code>tarask</code> for Taraškievica</li>
<li><a href="https://cbk-zam.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="cbk-zam:">cbk-zam:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chavacano" class="extiw" title="w:Chavacano">Zamboanga Chavacano</a> Wikipedia (note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/cbk">cbk</a></code> is the correct code for the larger family of langugages Zamboanga Chavacano is a member of)</li>
<li><a href="https://fiu-vro.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="fiu-vro:">fiu-vro:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V%C3%B5ro_language" class="extiw" title="w:Võro language">Võro</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/vro">vro</a></code> — note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/fiu">fiu</a></code> is the official code for the family of languages Võro is a member of)</li>
<li><a href="https://ksh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ksh:">ksh:</a> – code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ripuarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ripuarian language">Ripuarian</a> Wikipedia, even though <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/ksh">ksh</a></code> actually represents <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colognian" class="extiw" title="w:Colognian">Kölsch (or Colognian)</a>, a subset of Ripuarian</li>
<li><a href="https://map-bms.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="map-bms:">map-bms:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Banyumasan_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Banyumasan dialect">Banyumasan</a> Wikipedia (note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/map">map</a></code> does represent the family of languages the Banyumasan dialect falls within)</li>
<li><a href="https://nds-nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nds-nl:">nds-nl:</a> – invented code used for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a> Wikipedia would technically be the correct code for Low Saxon spoken in the Netherlands (i.e., <code>nds-NL</code>), but is therefore redundant with <a href="https://nds.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nds:">nds:</a>, the code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German/Low Saxon</a> Wikipedia (note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nds">nds</a></code> is the correct code for the Low German/Low Saxon family of languages, which Dutch Low Saxon is a member of)</li>
<li><a href="https://nrm.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nrm:">nrm:</a> – code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norman language">Norman</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nrf">nrf</a></code> — note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nrm">nrm</a></code> is the official code for the completely unrelated language <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narom_language" class="extiw" title="w:Narom language">Narom</a>)</li>
<li><a href="https://roa-rup.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="roa-rup:">roa-rup:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aromanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Aromanian language">Aromanian</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/rup">rup</a></code> — note that <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/roa">roa</a></code> is the standard code for the larger family of Romance languages that Aromanian is a member of)</li>
<li><a href="https://roa-tara.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="roa-tara:">roa-tara:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tarantino_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Tarantino dialect">Tarantino</a> Wikipedia (again, <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/roa">roa</a></code> is the standard code for the large family of Romance languages that the Tarantino dialect falls within)</li>
<li><a href="https://sh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="sh:">sh:</a> – deprecated code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/hbs">hbs</a></code>)</li>
<li><a href="https://simple.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="simple:">simple:</a> – invented code used for the Simple <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a> Wikipedia (which is just an IETF language tag, not the formal code <code>en-simple</code>)</li>
<li><a href="https://zh-classical.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-classical:">zh-classical:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Chinese">Classical Chinese</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/lzh">lzh</a></code>)</li>
<li><a href="https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-min-nan:">zh-min-nan:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min">Southern Min</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nan">nan</a></code>)</li>
<li><a href="https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-yue:">zh-yue:</a> – invented code used for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese">Cantonese</a> Wikipedia (not the official code <code><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/yue">yue</a></code>)</li></ol>
<p>Note that <a href="https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T172035" class="extiw" title="phab:T172035">renaming wiki subdomains is very difficult</a>, which is why so many of these nonstandard codes are still in use despite the existence of alternatives.
</p>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Redirects-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Redirects"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Redirects-Other_Wikipedias"></span><span id="Redirects:"></span> Redirects<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Redirects-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<ol><li><a href="https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="be-x-old:">be-x-old:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="be-tarask:">be-tarask:</a> (see above section)</li>
<li><a href="https://cs.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="cz:">cz:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://cs.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="cs:">cs:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a> Wikipedia)</li>
<li><a href="https://da.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="dk:">dk:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://da.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="da:">da:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a> Wikipedia)</li>
<li><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="jp:">jp:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ja:">ja:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a> Wikipedia)</li>
<li><a href="https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mo:">mo:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://ro.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ro:">ro:</a> (as discussed <a href="#Deleted_Wikipedias_now_hosted_elsewhere">above</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Moldovan language">Moldovan</a> Wikipedia now redirects to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a> Wikipedia)</li>
<li><a href="https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nan:">nan:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-min-nan:">zh-min-nan:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min_language" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min language">Southern Min</a> Wikipedia)</li>
<li><a href="https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nb:">nb:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="no:">no:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a> Wikipedia using <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Bokmål orthography</a>)</li>
<li><a href="https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="yue:">yue:</a> – redirects to <a href="https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-yue:">zh-yue:</a> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese language">Cantonese</a> Wikipedia)</li></ol>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Non-language_subdomains-Other_Wikipedias"><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-language_subdomains"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Non-language_subdomains-Other_Wikipedias"></span>Non-language subdomains<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Non-language_subdomains-Other_Wikipedias"></span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="https://nostalgia.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="nostalgia:">nostalgia:</a> – A read-only snapshot of Wikipedia's early days.</li>
<li><a href="//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sep11wiki" class="extiw" title="sep11:">sep11:</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Sep11wiki" title="Sep11wiki">Sep11wiki</a> existed with a .wikipedia.org URL from 2001 to 2008, despite its totally different scope and purpose from all other Wikipedias. It was made read-only in 2006 and closed two years later.</li>
<li><a href="https://ten.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="tenwiki:">ten:</a> – Used for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_10" title="Wikipedia 10">Wikipedia 10</a>, the 10th anniversary of Wikipedia celebration events. (Since "<a href="https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/ten" class="extiw" title="iso639-3:ten">ten</a>" is an ISO language code for the extinct <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tama_language_(Colombia)" class="extiw" title="w:Tama language (Colombia)">Tama language in Colombia</a>, the interwiki prefix "<a href="https://ten.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="tenwiki:">tenwiki:</a>" is now used to refer to this site.)</li></ul>
</section><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2 ext-discussiontools-init-section section-heading" onclick="mfTempOpenSection(4)"><span class="indicator mf-icon mf-icon-expand mf-icon--small"></span><h2 data-mw-thread-id="h-See_also"><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-See_also"></span>See also<span data-mw-comment-end="h-See_also"></span></span></h2><!--__DTELLIPSISBUTTON__{"threadItem":{"headingLevel":2,"name":"h-","type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-See_also","replies":["h-Additional_resources_and_statistics-See_also","h-Additional_projects-See_also"]}}--></div><section class="mf-section-4 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-4">

<li><a href="/wiki/There_is_also_a_Wikipedia_in_your_language" title="There is also a Wikipedia in your language">There is also a Wikipedia in your language</a></li></ul>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Additional_resources_and_statistics-See_also"><span class="mw-headline" id="Additional_resources_and_statistics"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Additional_resources_and_statistics-See_also"></span>Additional resources and statistics<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Additional_resources_and_statistics-See_also"></span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Abstract_Wikipedia" title="Abstract Wikipedia">Abstract Wikipedia</a> – An upcoming Wikimedia project.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Administrators_of_Wikimedia_projects/Wikipedias" title="Administrators of Wikimedia projects/Wikipedias">Administrators of Wikimedia projects/Wikipedias</a> – with the numbers of users</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Help:Interwiki_linking#Interlanguage_links" title="Help:Interwiki linking">Interlanguage links</a> – MediaWiki software feature</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_wikis" title="List of largest wikis">List of largest wikis</a> – Only Includes Lists of the largest wikis</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Requests_for_new_languages" title="Requests for new languages">Requests for new languages</a> – A Proposal Used for new language versions.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects" title="Proposals for closing projects">Proposals for closing projects</a> – A Proposal used for Closing or Deleting the wikimedia projects.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Proposals_for_new_projects" title="Proposals for new projects">Proposals for new projects</a> – A Proposal used for new wikimedia projects.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias/logarithmic_chart" title="List of Wikipedias/logarithmic chart">List of Wikipedias/logarithmic chart</a> – updated with {{<a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Template:NUMBEROF/data" title="Special:MyLanguage/Template:NUMBEROF/data">NUMBEROF/data</a>}}</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias/sortable" title="List of Wikipedias/sortable">List of Wikipedias/sortable</a> – similar to tables here but in a single table for easier sorting</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Meta:Templates_for_translating_language_names" title="Meta:Templates for translating language names">Meta:Templates for translating language names</a> – mostly deprecated by new features of the software</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Multilingual_Wikipedia" title="Multilingual Wikipedia">Multilingual Wikipedia</a> – A content page about the Communication of Wikipedia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix" title="Special:SiteMatrix">Special:SiteMatrix</a> – automatically generated table of languages for all projects (including wikis not yet created), ordered by language code</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Template:Active_Wikipedias" title="Template:Active Wikipedias">Template:Active Wikipedias</a> – just a list of all existing Wikipedias (with links) ordered by local language name</li>
<li><a href="https://iw.toolforge.org/pageviews" class="extiw" title="toolforge:pageviews">Wikipedia article traffic stats</a> – counts hits (views) for individual articles</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_logo_in_each_language" title="Wikipedia logo in each language">Wikipedia logo in each language</a>, including the name "Wikipedia" in different languages</li>
<li><a href="https://stats.wikimedia.org/" class="extiw" title="stats:">Wikimedia Statistics</a> – several statistical metrics for all Wikimedia projects</li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Multilingual_coordination" class="extiw" title="w:Wikipedia:Multilingual coordination">Wikipedia:Multilingual coordination</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_milestones" title="Wikipedia milestones">Wikipedia milestones</a> (+<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Milestone_statistics" class="extiw" title="en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics">en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedias_in_multiple_writing_systems" title="Wikipedias in multiple writing systems">Wikipedias in multiple writing systems</a></li></ul>
<h3 data-mw-thread-id="h-Additional_projects-See_also"><span class="mw-headline" id="Additional_projects"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Additional_projects-See_also"></span>Additional projects<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Additional_projects-See_also"></span></span></h3>
